\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02521}02521     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} OptimizeConstantMath1()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02522}02522     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02523}02523         \textcolor{comment}{// This optimization does three things:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02524}02524         \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ For adding groups:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02525}02525         \textcolor{comment}{//          Constants are added together.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02551}02551             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02552}02552 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            \#define ConstantUnaryFun(token, fun) \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02610}02610     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} OptimizeAddMulFlat()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02611}02611     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02612}02612         \textcolor{comment}{// This optimization flattens the topography of the tree.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02613}02613         \textcolor{comment}{//   Examples:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02614}02614         \textcolor{comment}{//       x + (y+z) = x+y+z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02615}02615         \textcolor{comment}{//       x * (y/z) = x*y/z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02616}02616         \textcolor{comment}{//       x / (y/z) = x/y*z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02617}02617 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02722}02722     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} OptimizeLogarithm()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02723}02723     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02724}02724         \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02725}02725 \textcolor{comment}{            This is basic logarithm math:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02726}02726 \textcolor{comment}{              pow(X,Y)/log(Y) = X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02727}02727 \textcolor{comment}{              log(X)/log(Y) = logY(X)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02728}02728 \textcolor{comment}{              log(X\string^Y)      = log(X)*Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02729}02729 \textcolor{comment}{              log(X*Y)      = log(X)+log(Y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02730}02730 \textcolor{comment}{              exp(log(X)*Y) = X\string^Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02731}02731 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02732}02732 \textcolor{comment}{            This function does these optimizations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02733}02733 \textcolor{comment}{               pow(const\_E, log(x))   = x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02734}02734 \textcolor{comment}{               pow(const\_E, log(x)*y) = x\string^y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02735}02735 \textcolor{comment}{               pow(10,      log(x)*const\_L10I*y) = x\string^y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02736}02736 \textcolor{comment}{               pow(z,       log(x)/log(z)*y)     = x\string^y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02737}02737 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02738}02738 \textcolor{comment}{            And this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02739}02739 \textcolor{comment}{               log(x\string^z)             = z * log(x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02740}02740 \textcolor{comment}{            Which automatically causes these too:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02741}02741 \textcolor{comment}{               log(pow(const\_E, x))         = x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02742}02742 \textcolor{comment}{               log(pow(y,       x))         = x * log(y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02743}02743 \textcolor{comment}{               log(pow(pow(const\_E, y), x)) = x*y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02744}02744 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02745}02745 \textcolor{comment}{            And it does this too:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02746}02746 \textcolor{comment}{               log(x) + log(y) + log(z) = log(x * y * z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02747}02747 \textcolor{comment}{               log(x * exp(y)) = log(x) + y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02748}02748 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02749}02749 \textcolor{comment}{        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02750}02750 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{fparser_8cc_source_l02751}02751         \textcolor{comment}{// Must be already in exponential form.}}
